<p><a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" class="external text" href="https://letsplay.live/games/dota2/">Let's Play Live</a> returns with season 3 of <b>LPL Pro 2020</b>, with teams from Oceania and Southeast Asia competing for a total prize pool of $5,000 <abbr title="Australian Dollar">AUD</abbr>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=LetsPlayLive/2020/ANZ_Championship/Season_3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Group Stage</b>
<ul><li>Single round-robin</li>
<li>All matches are played in a <abbr title="Best-of-two">Bo2</abbr></li>
<li>Top four advance to playoffs</li></ul></li>
<li><b>Playoffs</b>
<ul><li>Single-elimination bracket</li>
<li>Semifinals are <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr> while Grand Final is <abbr title="Best-of-five">Bo5</abbr></li></ul></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Broadcast_Talent">Broadcast Talent</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=LetsPlayLive/2020/ANZ_Championship/Season_3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Broadcast Talent">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Commentators:</b>
<ul><li><span class="flag"><a href="/dota2/Category:Australia" title="Australia"><img alt="Australia" src="/commons/images/a/a3/Au_hd.png" width="36" height="24" loading="lazy" /></a></span>&#160;<a href="/dota2/index.php?title=GTH&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="GTH (page does not exist)">GTH</a>&#160;(Ryan Lindeberg)</li>
<li><span class="flag"><a href="/dota2/Category:New_Zealand" title="New Zealand"><img alt="New Zealand" src="/commons/images/8/8a/Nz_hd.png" width="36" height="24" loading="lazy" /></a></span>&#160;<a href="/dota2/Fury_(Sam_Johnson)" title="Fury (Sam Johnson)">Fury</a>&#160;(Sam Johnson)</li></ul></li></ul>
